These are formatted for forum use. [img=https://retroachievements.org/Images/labels/linkedfiles.png'] can 
be posted at the top of the list. Roms used to make the set can be labeled using 
[img=https://retroachievements.org/Images/labels/main.png] Standard placement is between the [b] 
and the filename. Entries that have more than one rom linked may be numbered for 
clarity. You may look up existing forum posts for reference.
